SELECT
	menu_code
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 1
	AND menu_code NOT IN (
		'sys-pivot',
		'dsmc-business-manage',
		'dsmc-compliance-result',
		'dsmc-compliance-strategy',
		'dsmc-compliance-task',
		'dsmc-compliance-template',
		'dsmc-controls-strategy',
		'dsmc-data-asset-app',
		'dsmc-data-asset-database',

	menu_code
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0

SELECT
	menu_code
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'

	menu_code
FROM
	ums_sys_menus

	application = 'dsm_web'

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'
	AND menu_code NOT IN (
		'sys-pivot',

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'
	AND menu_code NOT IN (

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'
	AND menu_code NOT IN (
		'sys-pivot',

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'
	AND menu_code IN (

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code REGEXP '^(dsmcp-|dsmc-|idm-|sdd-)'
	AND menu_code IN (
		'sys-pivot',

SELECT
	menu_code, menu_name
FROM
	ums_sys_menus
WHERE
	application = 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_category = 0
	AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^(dsmcp-|dsmc-|idm-|sdd-)'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'
	AND menu_code IN (
		'sys-pivot',

SELECT
    *
FROM
    ums_sys_menus
WHERE
    application = 'dsm_web'
  AND menu_category = 0
  AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
	AND menu_code REGEXP '^(dsmcp-|dsmc-|idm-|sdd-)'
	AND menu_code NOT REGEXP '^dsm-'

    menu_code
FROM
    ums_sys_menus
WHERE
    application = 'dsm_web'
  AND menu_category = 0
  AND menu_code != 'dsm_web'
